cmake-doc in Fedora 33

This page displays detailed information for a specific version of cmake-doc. You might want go back to the main page of cmake-doc.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-09-30 Björn Esser - 3.18.3-1 - Update to 3.18.3 - Explicitly require make - Add patch to support FlexiBLAS
2020-09-29 Christoph Junghans - 3.18.2-2 - Make cd "armv7hl-redhat-linux-gnueabi" /usr/bin/ctest --output-on-failure --force-new-ctest-process -j5 --verbose non-verbose by default cd -
2020-08-20 Björn Esser - 3.18.2-1 - Update to 3.18.2
2020-08-01 Björn Esser - 3.18.1-1 - Update to 3.18.1
2020-07-29 Orion Poplawski - 3.18.0-5 - Handle arguments for ctest3 macro
2020-07-27 Fedora Release Engineering - 3.18.0-4 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_33_Mass_Rebuild
2020-07-22 Björn Esser - 3.18.0-3 - Default to --verbose for ctest as well
2020-07-19 Neal Gompa - 3.18.0-2 - Make in-source builds behave like before
2020-07-18 Igor Raits - 3.18.0-1.1 - Enable out-of-source builds by default
2020-07-16 Björn Esser - 3.18.0-1 - Update to 3.18.0
